***vluchtelingenkamp.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vluchtelingenkamp.html>vluchtelingenkamp</a> (27880)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vluchteling.html>vluchteling</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamp.html>kamp</a></i>, probably a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">refugee camp</i>. First attested around 1900 in relation to the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Second_Boer_War" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Second Boer War">Second <a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>Boer</a> War</a>, denoting the British internment/concentration camps. As a result it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> initially considered a cynical, sanitised term, but the word became more neutral during the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_World_War" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:First World War">First World War</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vluchtelingenkamp.html>vluchtelingenkamp</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vluchtelingenkampen.html>vluchtelingenkampen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vluchtelingenkamp.html>vluchtelingenkampje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>refugee camp</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vluchtelingenkamp.html>vluchtelingenkamp</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:kamp.html>kamp</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijdelijke.html>tijdelijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opvang.html>opvang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vluchtelingen.html>vluchtelingen</a></li></ol>

***vluchtig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vluchtig.html>vluchtig</a> (17425)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vluchten.html>vluchten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flee, escape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vluchtig.html>vluchtig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vluchtig.html>vluchtiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">vluchtigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>volatile (evaporating readily)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vluchtig.html>Vluchtige</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoffen.html>stoffen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lucht.html>lucht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blootgesteld.html>blootgesteld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdampen.html>verdampen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:snel.html>snel</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Volatile</b> substances that are exposed to air evaporate quickly.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>superficial <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">shallow, not thorough</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vluchtig.html>vluchtig</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderzoek.html>onderzoek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vliegtuig.html>vliegtuig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bracht.html>bracht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> defect <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A <b>superficial</b> examination of the aircraft <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> not reveal a defect.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fleeting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geluk.html>Geluk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:duurt.html>duurt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vluchtig.html>vluchtig</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ogenblik.html>ogenblik</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Happiness lasts for only a <b>fleeting</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***vocht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vocht.html>vocht</a> (3306)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vucht</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vocht.html>vocht</a></i>. Substantivized form of an identical adjective, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fuhti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">humid, <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a>, damp; marsh-like</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*funhtijaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">humid, <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a>, damp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. In Middle Dutch the word gradually shifted from being an adjective to being a noun, with the old adjective being replaced by <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vochtig.html>vochtig</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">humid, <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fuht</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">moist, damp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">feucht</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a>, humid, damp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vocht.html>vocht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>dampness, moisture</li>
<li>liquid</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vocht.html>vocht</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vocht.html>vochter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">vochtst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">moist</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vochtig.html>vochtig</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vochtigheid.html>vochtigheid</a> (21458)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vochtig.html>vochtig</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a> (12418)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voeden.html>voeden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to feed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ing, -ion, -ment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***voegen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:voegen.html>voegen</a> (5760)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:voegen.html>voegen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fuogen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fōgijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voegen.html>voegen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to place, to put</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to add</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to grout</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fit, to suit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:voegt.html>voegt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>suit</b> you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>

***voelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:voelen.html>voelen</a> (682)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:voelen.html>voelen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fuolen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fōlijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voelen.html>voelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to feel, to have sensation of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:voel.html>Voel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> wind <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haren.html>haren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruisen.html>ruist</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you <b>feel</b> the wind that <a href = vnd.unilang:rushes.html>rushes</a> through your hair?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to feel, to experience a feeling
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:voel.html>voel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>feel</b> so good.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:voelen.html>voelen</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:overgankelijk.html>overgankelijk</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewaarworden.html>gewaarworden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanraking.html>aanraking</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:meestal.html>meestal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:betrekking.html>betrekking</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:temperatuur.html>temperatuur</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:druk.html>druk</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:voelde.html>voelde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a> hard <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achterhoofd.html>achterhoofd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanvliegen.html>aanvloog</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd>
<dd><span style="color:0060ff;font-weight: bold;">▸</span> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:terwijl.html>Terwijl</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goedkeurend.html>goedkeurend</a> ***voer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:voer.html>voer</a> (2693)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voeder.html>voeder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:voeder.html>voeder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fuoder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fōdrą</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*peh₂-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voer.html>voer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>fodder, <a href = vnd.unilang:grub.html>grub</a>, animal food, (for humans) inferior food</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bait</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voeden.html>voeden</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voeder.html>voeder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:voeder.html>voeder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fuothar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fōþrą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voer.html>voer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>(wagon) load</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a wine measure, about a barrel</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voer.html>voer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voeren.html>voeren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voer.html>voertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:voeren.html>voeren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fuoren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fōrijaną</i>, causative of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*faraną</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:varen.html>varen</a></i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wage <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">war</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>A contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voederen.html>voederen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:voederen.html>voederen</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:voeder.html>voeder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lining</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fōdrą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sheath</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***voet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:voet.html>voet</a> (1350)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:voet.html>voet</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fuot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fōts</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pṓds</i>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">foot</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">lowest part of the <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">foot</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">most basic element of a metre</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***vogel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vogel.html>vogel</a> (1919)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vōgel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fogal</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">vogal</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fuglaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vogel.html>vogel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vogels.html>vogels</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">vogelen</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vogeltje.html>vogeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">vogelijn</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bird, any member of the class <a href = vnd.unilang:aves.html>Aves</a></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:gaai.html>gaai</a>, a feathered target in archery or shooting</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A dude, <span class="Latn" lang="en">cat</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vogel.html>vogel</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> one of the few <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> where the obsolete Dutch diminutive <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijn</i> can still be encountered: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vogelijn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">little bird</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> chiefly poetic and can be found in poems and <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>songs</a>, but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not often used elsewhere.
</p>

***vol.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a> (459)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fol</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ful</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fullaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pl̥h₁nós</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voller.html>voller</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">volst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>full, replete
